<Tag slot="tag">

<TagTitle slot="title">

# Client Search Endpoints

</TagTitle>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/adminsearch \{#operation-adminsearch\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Search the index (admin)_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieves results for search query without respect for permissions. This is available only to privileged users.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-adminsearch+code-samples+typescript">

TypeScript

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-adminsearch+code-samples+typescript">

<TryItNow
  dependencyUrlPrefix="/try-it-now"
  defaultValue="import { Glean } from &quot;@gleanwork/api-client&quot;;&NewLine;&NewLine;const glean = new Glean({&NewLine;  apiToken: &quot;GLEAN_API_TOKEN&quot;,&NewLine;});&NewLine;&NewLine;async function run() {&NewLine;  const result = await glean.client.search.queryAsAdmin({&NewLine;    trackingToken: &quot;trackingToken&quot;,&NewLine;    pageSize: 10,&NewLine;    query: &quot;vacation policy&quot;,&NewLine;    requestOptions: {&NewLine;      facetFilters: [&NewLine;        {&NewLine;          fieldName: &quot;type&quot;,&NewLine;          values: [&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;article&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;document&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;          ],&NewLine;        },&NewLine;        {&NewLine;          fieldName: &quot;department&quot;,&NewLine;          values: [&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;engineering&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;          ],&NewLine;        },&NewLine;      ],&NewLine;      facetBucketSize: 421489,&NewLine;    },&NewLine;  });&NewLine;&NewLine;  console.log(result);&NewLine;}&NewLine;&NewLine;run();&NewLine;"
  packageName="@gleanwork/api-client"
/>

</SectionContent>

</TabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### hasCopyPaste \{#operation-adminsearch+request+inputdetails+searchrequestinputdetails+hascopypaste\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Whether the associated query was at least partially copy-pasted.  If subsequent requests are issued after a copy-pasted query is constructed (e.g. with facet modifications), this bit should continue to be set for those requests.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableBreakoutProperties>

</ExpandableBreakout>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="maxSnippetSize"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+maxsnippetsize"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### maxSnippetSize \{#operation-adminsearch+request+maxsnippetsize\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hint to the server about how many characters long a snippet may be. Server may return less or more.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
400
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="pageSize"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+pagesize"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### pageSize \{#operation-adminsearch+request+pagesize\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hint to the server about how many results to send back. Server may return less or more. Structured results and clustered results don't count towards pageSize.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
100
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="query"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+query"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"required","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### query \{#operation-adminsearch+request+query\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The search terms.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
vacation policy
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty

  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+datasourcefilter"
  parentId="requestOptions_SearchRequestOptions"

  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### datasourceFilter \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+datasourcefilter\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Filter results to a single datasource name (e.g. gmail, slack). All results are returned if missing.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_SearchRequestOptions_datasourcesFilter"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+datasourcesfilter"
  parentId="requestOptions_SearchRequestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"string","children":[{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### datasourcesFilter \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+datasourcesfilter\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Filter results to one or more datasources (e.g. gmail, slack). All results are returned if missing.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_SearchRequestOptions_defaultFacets"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+defaultfacets"
  parentId="requestOptions_SearchRequestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"string","children":[{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### defaultFacets \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+defaultfacets\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Facets for which FacetResults should be fetched and that don't apply to a particular datasource. If specified, these values will replace the standard default facets (last_updated_at, from, etc.). The requested facets will be returned alongside datasource-specific facets if searching a single datasource.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### disableQueryAutocorrect \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+disablequeryautocorrect\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Disables automatic adjustment of the input query for spelling corrections or other reasons.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### facetFilterSets \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+facetfiltersets\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of facet filter sets that will be OR'ed together. SearchRequestOptions where both facetFilterSets and facetFilters set are considered as bad request. Callers should set only one of these fields.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### facetFilters \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+facetfilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### fetchAllDatasourceCounts \{#operation-adminsearch+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+fetchalldatasourcecounts\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hints that the QE should return result counts (via the datasource facet result) for all supported datasources, rather than just those specified in the datasource[s]Filter

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"

  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-adminsearch+responses+200+application-json+facetresults+facetresult+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

For most facets this will be the empty string, meaning the facet is high-level and applies to all documents for the datasource. When non-empty, this is used to group facets together (i.e. group facets for each doctype for a certain datasource)

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Service Cloud
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### rewrittenFacetFilters \{#operation-adminsearch+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  expandByDefault={false}

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-adminsearch+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-adminsearch+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/autocomplete \{#operation-autocomplete\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Autocomplete_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve query suggestions, operators and documents for the given partially typed query.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-autocomplete+code-samples+typescript">

</SectionTab>

##### datasourcesFilter \{#operation-autocomplete+request+datasourcesfilter\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### tabId \{#operation-autocomplete+responses+200+application-json+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+tabid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A unique id for all requests a user makes from a given tab, no matter how far apart. A new tab id is only generated when a user issues a request from a new tab.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/feed \{#operation-feed\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Feed of documents and events_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

The personalized feed/home includes different types of contents including suggestions, recents, calendar events and many more.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-feed+responses+200+application-json+facetresults+facetresult+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

For most facets this will be the empty string, meaning the facet is high-level and applies to all documents for the datasource. When non-empty, this is used to group facets together (i.e. group facets for each doctype for a certain datasource)

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/recommendations \{#operation-recommendations\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Recommend documents_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve recommended documents for the given URL or Glean Document ID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

##### pageSize \{#operation-recommendations+request+pagesize\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### sessionTrackingToken \{#operation-recommendations+responses+200+application-json+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+sessiontrackingtoken\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A unique token for this session. A new session (and token) is created when the user issues a request from a new tab or when our server hasn't seen activity for more than 10 minutes from a tab.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="sessionInfo_SessionInfo_tabId"
  headingId="operation-recommendations+responses+200+application-json+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+tabid"
  parentId="sessionInfo_SessionInfo"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### tabId \{#operation-recommendations+responses+200+application-json+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+tabid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A unique id for all requests a user makes from a given tab, no matter how far apart. A new tab id is only generated when a user issues a request from a new tab.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/search \{#operation-search\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Search_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve results from the index for the given query and filters.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-search+code-samples+typescript">

TypeScript

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-search+code-samples+typescript">

<TryItNow
  dependencyUrlPrefix="/try-it-now"
  defaultValue="import { Glean } from &quot;@gleanwork/api-client&quot;;&NewLine;&NewLine;const glean = new Glean({&NewLine;  apiToken: &quot;GLEAN_API_TOKEN&quot;,&NewLine;});&NewLine;&NewLine;async function run() {&NewLine;  const result = await glean.client.search.query({&NewLine;    trackingToken: &quot;trackingToken&quot;,&NewLine;    pageSize: 10,&NewLine;    query: &quot;vacation policy&quot;,&NewLine;    requestOptions: {&NewLine;      facetFilters: [&NewLine;        {&NewLine;          fieldName: &quot;type&quot;,&NewLine;          values: [&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;article&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;document&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;          ],&NewLine;        },&NewLine;        {&NewLine;          fieldName: &quot;department&quot;,&NewLine;          values: [&NewLine;            {&NewLine;              value: &quot;engineering&quot;,&NewLine;              relationType: &quot;EQUALS&quot;,&NewLine;            },&NewLine;          ],&NewLine;        },&NewLine;      ],&NewLine;      facetBucketSize: 400611,&NewLine;    },&NewLine;  });&NewLine;&NewLine;  console.log(result);&NewLine;}&NewLine;&NewLine;run();&NewLine;"
  packageName="@gleanwork/api-client"
/>

</SectionContent>

</TabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

Whether the associated query was at least partially copy-pasted.  If subsequent requests are issued after a copy-pasted query is constructed (e.g. with facet modifications), this bit should continue to be set for those requests.

##### maxSnippetSize \{#operation-search+request+maxsnippetsize\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">


  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### pageSize \{#operation-search+request+pagesize\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hint to the server about how many results to send back. Server may return less or more. Structured results and clustered results don't count towards pageSize.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
100
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

##### defaultFacets \{#operation-search+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+defaultfacets\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Facets for which FacetResults should be fetched and that don't apply to a particular datasource. If specified, these values will replace the standard default facets (last_updated_at, from, etc.). The requested facets will be returned alongside datasource-specific facets if searching a single datasource.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### timezoneOffset \{#operation-search+request+requestoptions+searchrequestoptions+timezoneoffset\}

##### sessionTrackingToken \{#operation-search+request+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+sessiontrackingtoken\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

##### tabId \{#operation-search+request+sessioninfo+sessioninfo+tabid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A unique id for all requests a user makes from a given tab, no matter how far apart. A new tab id is only generated when a user issues a request from a new tab.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### groupName \{#operation-search+responses+200+application-json+facetresults+facetresult+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

For most facets this will be the empty string, meaning the facet is high-level and applies to all documents for the datasource. When non-empty, this is used to group facets together (i.e. group facets for each doctype for a certain datasource)

##### rewrittenFacetFilters \{#operation-search+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-search+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

  slot="entry"

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-search+responses+200+application-json+rewrittenfacetfilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
